$(document).ready(function () {
    var clearAllFilterCookies = function () {
        var cookies = document.cookie.split(";");
        for (var i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) {
            var cookie = cookies[i].split("=");
            var cookieName = $.trim(cookie[0]).toLowerCase();
            if (cookieName.indexOf("filter") === 0 || cookieName === "currentpage") {
                $.cookie(cookie[0], null, { path: "/" });
            }
        }
    };

    $("#menu-root a, form.inventory-quick-search button, div.ft a").click(function () {
        clearAllFilterCookies();
        return true;
    });

    if (window.location.pathname.toLowerCase().indexOf("consumersitemap") >= 0) {
        $("div.layout-sitemap a").click(function () {
            clearAllFilterCookies();
            return true;
        });
    }
});</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
          sortField = "sp";
          sortDir = "ascending";

          makeTitle = "Make";
          modelTitle = "Model";
          trimTitle = "Trim";

          area = "Apex";
          department = "Used";
          currentDepartmentId = "3";
          incentiveImage = "http://assets.clickmotive.com/designs/_Components/InventorySearch/InventoryIncentiveStar.png";


          certifiedLogoUrl = "";
          certifiedLogoTarget = "_blank";


          
            $(window).load(function() {
            $('#results').parent().find('div.section').toggle(true);
            });

            $(document).ready(function() {
            // Set up the current page:
            pageType = $('#pageType').val();
            design = $('#design').val();
            makeCount = $('#makeCount').val();
            filingName = $('#filingName').val();
            assetType = pageType == 'Network' ? 'Networks' : 'Customers';

            queryString = "p=3";

						pageTotal = parseInt($('#MaxPage').val());
						if (pageTotal < 1)
							pageTotal = 1;
						
						if (window.location.search.indexOf('page') != -1) {
						currentPage = parseInt($.query.get('page')); // +1;
						}
						else if($.cookie('currentPage')) {
						currentPage = parseInt($.cookie('currentPage'), 10);
						}
						else if ($.cookie('filterPage')) {
						var valueArray = $.cookie('filterPage').split('|');
						currentPage = parseInt(valueArray[valueArray.length - 1]);
						}

						if ($('#search-make1').val() != '') {
						updateQueryString('k', $('#search-make1').val());
						makeChanged($('#search-make1').val(), true);
						}

						if ($('#search-model1').val() != '') {
						updateQueryString('d', $('#search-model1').val());
						}

						if ($('#search-trim1').val() != '') {
						updateQueryString('trim', $('#search-trim1').val());
						}

						initQueryString('Dealership', 'filterDealership', 'Dealership', '0');
            initQueryString('MinMPG', 'filterFuelEfficiency1', 'FuelEfficiency1', '0');
            initQueryString('MaxMPG', 'filterFuelEfficiency2', 'FuelEfficiency2', '0');
            initQueryString('r', 'filterBodyStyle', 'BodyStyle', '');
            initQueryString('k', 'filterMake', 'Make', '');
            initQueryString('d', 'filterModel', 'Model', '');
            initQueryString('MinMSRP', 'filterPriceRange1', 'PriceRange1', '0');
            initQueryString('MaxMSRP', 'filterPriceRange2', 'PriceRange2', '0');
            initQueryString('trim', 'filterTrim', 'Trim', "");
            initQueryString('y', 'filterYear', 'Year', '0');
            initQueryString('SortExpression', '', '', '');

            var inventoryLayout = $('#layout-inventory');

            models = inventoryLayout.find('#hidden-models');

            recentSearchCount = inventoryLayout.find('#recent-searches li').length;
            window.setTimeout('rotateRecentSearch()', 3000);

            inventoryLayout
            .find('.search-filters .collapsible')
            .CM_Collapsible({
            speed: 500,
            collapsed: false
            });

            inventoryLayout
            .find('#inventory-view-list, #inventory-view-detail, #inventory-view-gallery')
            .bind("click", function(e) {
            var s = $(this).attr('title');
            switchInventoryView(s.replace(/ view/gi, ''));
            setMinMaxRows(currentPage);
            updatePage(currentPage);
            return false;
            });

            inventoryLayout.find("#compare-submit1").click(function() { getComparisonData(); return false; });
            inventoryLayout.find("#compare-submit2").click(function() { getComparisonData(); return false; });

            errorDialog = $('#comparison-error');
            errorDialog.dialog({ autoOpen: false, buttons: { "Ok": function() { $(this).dialog("close"); } } });


            $('#layout-inventory input[type=checkbox][name=compare]').click(function() {
            comparecheck(this);
            });

            customerZipCode = $.cookie('CustomerZipCode');
            updateZip(customerZipCode);


            


            setMinMaxRows(currentPage);
            updatePage(currentPage);

            });

          </script>
